ExecutionPlan\\n   - Rules include node elimination, index usage, join reordering, and other optimizations\\n   - Generates potentially multiple execution plans and selects the best one\\n   - optimized plan\\n   - Instantiates ExecutionBlock instances for each node in the plan\\n   - Sets up data flow pipelines between blocks\\n   - Manages item block memory and coordinates block execution\\n\\n4. **Execution Phase** (arangod/Aql/ExecutionBlock.cpp, ExecutionBlock class)\\n   - Base class for all execution blocks (filters, projections, data source scanning, etc.)\\n   - Each
